3 Resource Usage

Note: This resource usage calculation assumes that the "Boolean" data type is based on uint8 base type.
Further on padding bytes for structs are not considered, which depends on the compiler settings.

RAM Size: 1782253 Bytes
CONST Size: 49595 Bytes
